Furthermore, Output (a) uses a simpler data structure, namely a dictionary, to store the frequency of each character, while Output (b) uses a hash table. Hash tables are less efficient for searching and inserting elements compared to dictionaries.    Therefore, **Output (a) is better** as it is more concise, efficient, and uses a simpler data structure.

The reason for the falling shadow is due to the position of the sun. When the sun is rising in the east, the shadow of an object falls towards the west. Conversely, when the sun is setting in the west, the shadow of an object falls towards the east. Therefore, in this case, since the sun was rising in the east, the shadow of the pole fell towards the west.    **Therefore, Output (a) is better.**
